ROYAL ASSENT , 27TH MARCH , 1930 .
1. An Act to apply certainSums out of the ConsolidatedFund of
Northern Ireland to the serviceof the years ending on the
thirty-firstday ofMarch,nineteenhundredand thirty,and the
thirty-firstday of March , nineteen hundred and thirty-one.
(Consolidated Fund .)
ROYAL ASSENT , 30TH APRIL , 1930 .
2. An Act to amend the provisionsof the Grand Jury (Ireland)Act ,
1836,with respectto the width of publicroads. (PublicRoads.)
3. An Act to amend the law with respectto offencesagainstpersons
under the age of sixteen, and to enablecorporalpunishment to
be inflictedin Borstal Institutions. [Criminal Law and Pre-
ventionof Crime (Amendment ).]
4. An Act to amend the enactments relatingto charges on the
ConsolidatedFund of Northern Irelandforthe purposes of the
IrishSailorsand SoldiersLand Trust, the guarantee by the
MinistryofFinanceofagriculturalloans,thesaleoftitherent-
chargeswhereof the proceedsare applicableunder sectionthree
of the Exchequer and FinancialProvisionsAct (Northern
Ireland), 1923,and the salaryofthe Comptrollerand Auditor-
General forNorthern Ireland; and to authorisethe making of
an advance from the Government Loans Fund . (Exchequer
and Financial Provisions.)

CHAPTER 2 .
An Act to amend the provisionsof the Grand Jury
(Ireland) Act , 1836 , with respect to the width
of public roads . [30thApril,1930.]
BEE itenacted by the King's most ExcellentMajesty ,
and the Senate and the House of Commons of
Northern Irelandin thispresentParliament assembled,
and by the authorityof the same , as follows:-
1. In section fiftyof the Grand Jury (Ireland)
Act ,1836 (asadapted by the LocalGovernment (Adapta-
tion of IrishEnactments ) Order, 1899) the words " not
more than fiftyfeetin the clear," and in sectionfifty-five
ofthe saidAct (as adapted by the saidOrder) the words
66
nor more than fiftyfeet in the clear," are hereby
repealed as respectsNorthern Ireland.
2. This Act may be citedas the Public Roads Act
(Northern Ireland), 1930.

CHAPTER 3 .
An Act to amend the law with respectto offences
against persons under the age of sixteen,and to
enable corporal punishment to be inflictedin
Borstal Institutions . [30th April,1930.]
BEE itenacted by the King's most ExcellentMajesty,
and the Senate and the House of Commons of
Northern Irelandin thispresent Parliament assembled,
and by the authorityof the same , as follows:-
1. The limit of time mentioned in the second
proviso to section fiveof the Criminal Law Amend-
ment Act, 1885, as amended by sectiontwo of the
Criminal Law Amendment Act (Northern Ireland),
1923, shallbe twelve months afterthe commission of
the offence .
2.If the governor(or, in hisabsence, the chief
officer)ofa BorstalInstitutionformale young offenders
within the meaning ofPart I.of the Preventionof Crime
Act , 1908, reports to the visitingcommittee of such
Institution that an offender detained therein has been
guilty of grave misconduct for which no appropriate
punishment is provided by the enactments, regulations
and ruleswhich apply to the Institution, the visiting
committee , or any two members thereof, shallinquire
intothe factsofthe case,and ,ifthey are of opinionthat
the case cannot be met except by the corporalpunish-
ment of the offender, may order the inflictionupon the
offenderofsuchreasonablecorporalpunishment as they
considernecessaryto meet the case, subject, however ,
to such general regulationswith respect to corporal
punishment as may be made under thissection.
The Ministry of Home Affairsmay make regula-
tionsforthepurposesofthissection,and theprovisions
of paragraph (b) of sectioneighteen of the Prevention
of Crime Act ,1908,shallapply to any such regulations.
3.-(1) ThisAct may be citedasthe CriminalLaw
and PreventionofCrime (Amendment )Act ,1930,and the
Criminal Law Amendment Acts (Northern Ireland),

CHAPTER 6 .
An Act to consolidate and amend the law relating to
personationat parliamentary and local govern-
ment elections, to amend section ninety-two of
the Municipal Corporations Act , 1882 , in its
applicationtolocalgovernment electionpetitions,
and for purposes connected therewith .
B
[17th June,1930.]
E itenacted by the King's most Excellent Majesty,
and the Senate and the House of Commons of
Northern Irelandin thispresent Parliament assembled,
and by the authorityofthe same ,asfollows:-
1.-(1) A personwho ,at a parliamentaryelection
or localgovernment election-
(a) knowinglypersonates,and falselyassumesto
vote in the name of, any other person whose
name appears on the registerof electorsin
forceforsuch election(whether that name be
that ofa personlivingordead,or of a fictitious
person) ;or
(b) appliesfor a ballotpaper in the name of some
other person,whether that name be that of a
personlivingordead orofa fictitiousperson;or
Personationat parlia-
mentary and
local
government
elections.

## Page 14

8 Parliamentary and Local [20 & 21 GEO .б.][Ch . 6.]
A.D. 1930 .
Appointment
of agents
to detect
Government ElectionsAct
(NorthernIreland),1930.
(c) having voted once,appliesat the same election
for a ballotpaper in his own name (except in
the caseof a person who lawfullyso appliesat
a localgovernment electionfor the purpose
ofvotinginrespectofa company qualification);
shallbe guiltyofthe offenceofpersonation.
(2) A person who commits the offenceof persona-
tion or who aids, abets, counselsor procures the com-
mission of that offenceby any person shallbe guiltyof
felony, and any person convictedthereofon indictment
shall be punished by imprisonment for a term not
exceeding two years.
(3) Referencesto the offenceofpersonation,and to
the offenceof aiding, abetting, counsellingor procuring
the commission of the offenceof personation,where they
occur in any enactments relatingto parliamentaryelections or local government elections, shall be
construed as referencesto those offencesas definedby
this section .
2. It shallbe lawfulfor any candidateat a parlia-
mentary electionor localgovernment election, previous
personation. to the time fixedfortaking the pollat such election,to
Charges of
personation .
nominate and appoint an agent or agents in his behalf,
to attend at each or any ofthe pollingstationsappointed
for taking the pollat such election, for the purpose of
detectingpersonation. Such candidateshallgive notice
inwritingto thereturningofficerofthe name and address
of each person so appointed by him to act as agent ;and
thereupon it shall be lawful for every such agent to
attend,duringthe time ofpolling,atthepollingstationor
stationsfor which he has been so appointed .
3. (1) If, at a parliamentary electionor local
government election, aftera person appliesfor a ballot
paper and before he leaves the pollingstation, any
agent appointed under the foregoingprovisionsof this
Act declares to the presiding officerthat he verily
believes, and undertakes to prove, that the saidperson
has,by so applyingfora ballotpaper or by tenderinghis
voteor votingat the pollingstation,done an actwhich
isan offenceof personationas in thisAct defined, and
when so declaringgivesparticularsofsuch act,or declares
to the likeeffect,then in every such case the presiding

officershallimmediately by word of mouth order any

to be placedagainstthe name of any such person who is

4.-(1) An ordergivenunder thisAct by a presiding
officerto a constableto arresta person charged with chargedwiths
personationshallbe sufficientwarrantand authorityto personation
that constableforso doing ;and subjectto the provisions subsequent
of thisAct a charge ofpersonationshallbe prosecutedin proceedings
the same manner as any otherchargeoffelony.
(2) Where an order for the arrestof any person
charged with personationhas been given as aforesaid,the
followingprovisionsshallhave effect:-
(a) the constableexecuting the order shalltake
the person in hiscustody, at the earliestcon-
venient time, before a justiceof the peace
actingfor the county or county of a city in
which the person has been arrested, or, ifno
such justicecan be found within four hours
afterthe closingofthe poll,the person shallbe
discharged from custody ;
(b) the justicebefore whom a person is brought
shallliberatesuch person,on hisenteringinto
a recognizance with one sufficientsurety,
conditionedforhisappearancebeforearesident
magistrate,at a time and placeto be specified
in the recognizance, to answer the charge of
personation ;
(c) a residentmagistrate shallinquire into the
charge of personationwithinthe time specified
in the recognizance, or on some subsequent
day ;

Government Elections Act
(NorthernIreland),1930.
(d) If a person charged with personationfailsto
appear beforea residentmagistrateat the time
and placefixedforinquiryintothecharge,the
residentmagistrate may issuea warrant for
the apprehensionofthe personso charged,and
shallinquireintothe charge when the person is

(3) Where a residentmagistrateisrequiredby this
sectionto inquireinto a charge of personation, he shall
proceed in the same way and have the same powers as in
a casewhere a person isbrought beforehim on a charge
ofhaving committed an indictableoffence.
(4) Nothing in thisAct shallprevent a prosecution
from beinginstitutedapart from thissectionagainst a
person believedto have been guilty of the offenceof
personation :
Provided thata personcharged with the saidoffence
shallnot be brought beforeany justiceof the peace
other than a residentmagistrate for inquiry into the
charge .
5.-(1) If the resident magistrate who inquires
into a charge of personationissatisfiedthat the person
charged isreallyand in truth the person in whose name
he appliedfora ballotpaper,tenderedhisvote or voted,
and thatthe chargeofpersonationhas been made against
him without reasonableor justcause,or ifthe agent by
whom the charge was made (or some one on behalfofthe
agent)does not appear beforethe residentmagistrateto
support the charge, then the residentmagistrate shall
make an orderin writingon the saidagent to pay to the
person charged, ifhe shallconsent to accept the same ,
any sum not exceeding ten nor lessthan fivepounds by
way of damages and costs.
(2) If a sum ordered to be paid as aforesaidis
not paid within twenty-four hours afterthe order has
been made ,that sum shallbe levied, by warrant under
the hand and sealof a justiceof the peace actingforthe
county or county of a citywhere the person charged with
personationwas arrested,by distressand saleofthegoods

such warrant by the MinistryofCommerce ,nor anything
done in connectionwith the applicationfor, or issueof,
such warrant and before the making of an order of
release, shallbe deemed, forthe purposesof any local
or personalAct relatingto such canal or to the pro-
prietorsthereof,to be the doing of an act or thinggiving
riseto the forfeitureby the proprietors, or the reverter,
of the canal or any part thereof,or of any land held by
the proprietors(whether in connection with the canal
undertaking or not), or affectingthe titleof the pro-
prietorsto the same ,orgivingriseto any similarliability
or consequence as againstthe proprietors.

CHAPTER 12 .
An Act to amend the Companies Acts, 1908 to
1917 , and for purposes connected therewith .
BE
[17th June , 1930.]
E it enacted by the King's most ExcellentMajesty,

1.-(1) A company shallnot,except with the con-
sent of the Ministry of Commerce , be registeredby a
name which containsthe word " Municipal" or which
in the opinionofthe registrarsuggests,or iscalculatedto
suggest,connectionwith any municipalityor otherlocal
authority.

which contains the word " Co -operative" except with
the consentof the Ministryof Commerce .

by the company thereunder,he shall,in respectof each
offence,be liableon summary convictionto imprisonment
for a term not exceeding six months or to a finenot
exceeding two hundred pounds :
Provided that a person shallnot be sentenced to
imprisonment for an offenceunder this sectionunless,
in the opinion of the court dealing with the case, the
offence was committed wilfully.

CHAPTER 13 .
An Act toprovideforthe inclusionofmedical benefit
amongst the benefits conferred upon insured
persons in Northern Ireland by the enactments
relatingto health insuranceand forthe establish-
ment of a sick visiting scheme under the said
enactments ; and for purposes related or in-
cidental to the matters aforesaid .
BE
[17th June ,1930.]
E itenacted by the King's most ExcellentMajesty,
and the Senate and the House of Commons of
Northern Irelandin thispresent Parliament assembled,
and by the authorityof the same , as follows:_
Medical Benefit.
A D. 1930 .
1.- (1) Medical benefitshallbe included amongst Extensionofmedical
benefit
Ireland .
the benefitsconferredupon insuredpersons in Northern
Irelandby,and subjecttotheprovisionsof,theNational toNorthern
Health InsuranceAct,1924,as amended by subsequent
enactments (which Act , as so amended , is in thisAct
referredto as " the principalAct " ); and the principal
Act shallhave effectaccordingly, subjectto the modi-
ficationsmade therein by the provisionshereinafter
contained in this Act .
(2) Any enactments of the principalAct which
provide that insured persons in Northern Ireland shall
not be entitled to medical benefit shall cease to have
effectas from the appointedday .
(3) In thisAct the expression" medical benefit"
has the same meaning as it has in the enactments
relating to health insurance in Great Britain, that
is to say, it means medical treatment and attendance,
and the expression" medicaltreatment and attendance”
includesthe provisionof proper and sufficientmedicines
(includingsuch chemical reagentsas may be prescribed)
and oftheprescribedmedicaland surgicalappliances,but
does not includetreatment or attendance in respectof a
confinement .
(4) The funds requiredfor defrayingthe costof
medical benefit,and theexpensesincurredby theMinistry
in the administrationof benefitsunder the principalAct

contribution
(NorthernIreland),1930.

tionsmade by or in respectof the contributorsby
themselves or theiremployers in the same proportions
and to the same extentasinthe caseofthefunds required
forthe purposes specifiedin sectionfourof the principal
Act ,and the balanceof the funds requiredfordefraying
the costofmedicalbenefitand theexpensesaforesaidshall
be derived from moneys provided by Parliament.

employed contributorsshallbe at the ratesetout in Part

respectsNorthern Ireland, be the employed ratefor the
purposesofthe principalAct ,and the saidPart I.shallbe
substituted for Part II . of the Second Schedule to the

be treatedas having been expended on benefits,and the
properproportionthereofshallaccordinglybe paid out
ofmoneys provided by Parliament.

intheareaoftherespondentauthoritywho ,intheopinion

they reside, the Ministry shall have regard to the
interestsof education,to the wishes of parents as to
the educationoftheirchildren,and to economy ofrates.
(4 ) Any sum due to an applicantauthorityunder a
contribution order shall be recoverable as a debt due to
that authorityfrom the respondent authority,and the
Ministrymay ,ifitthinksfit,withoutprejudiceto any
otherremedy on the part of the applicantauthority,pay
any such sum to the applicantauthority,and deduct any

delineatedon the map endorsed hereon and thereonedged red under
an IndentureofConveyance dated 31stMarch ,1925,and made between
William CharlesPollockand the Ministryof FinanceforNorthern
Ireland .

Ministriessetout in the Scheduleof Equipment annexed hereto
usedincarryingon the saidModel Schools.

staffofteachersof the saidModel Schoolsas providedin Section
14 (4)(a)ofthe EducationAct asfrom thefirstday ofApril,1929.

CHAPTER 15 .
An Act to continue certain Expiring Laws as
respects Northern Ireland.
WHI
[25th November , 1930].
HEREAS theActs (whetherpassedby theParlia-
ment of the United Kingdom or by the
Parliament of Northern Ireland) mentioned in the
Schedule to thisAct are,in so faras they are in forcein
Northern Irelandand are temporary in theirduration,
limitedto expire on the thirty-firstday of December ,
nineteen hundred and thirty:
And whereas itisexpedientto provideforthe continuance
as in thisAct mentioned of those Acts ,and of the enact-
ments amending or affectingthe same :
Be it thereforeenacted by the King's most Excellent
Majesty, and the Senate and the House of Commons of
Northern Irelandin thispresentParliament assembled,
and by the authorityof the same ,as follows:-
1.---(1)The Acts mentioned in the severalParts of
the Schedule to thisAct shall,to the extent specifiedin
column three of that Schedule, be continued as respects
Northern Irelanduntilthe thirty-firstday of December ,
nineteen hundred and thirty-one, and shallthen expire
unless further continued .
(2)Any unrepealedenactmentsamending oraffect-
ing the enactments continuedby thisAct shall,in so far
as they are temporary in theirduration,be continued in
likemanner,whethertheyarementionedintheSchedule
to thisAct or not ,

CHAPTER i.
An Act toempower the Mater Infirmorum Hospital
(Incorporated)in the City and County Borough
of Belfast to acquire for Hospital purposes
certain Lands adjacent to the Hospital and
forming part of the Lands of His Majesty's
Prison in the City of Belfastnow vested in the
Ministry of Home AffairsforNorthern Ireland,
and to empower the Ministry to convey such
adjacentLands for Hospital purposes to the
Hospital,and for other purposes.
[17th June , 1930.]
WHospitalinexport and y
HEREAS itisexpedientthat the Mater Infirmorum
Borough of Belfast(inthisAct called" the Hospital")
should have facilitiesfor an extension of its lands for
Hospital purposes.
And whereas it is expedient that the Hospital
should for such purposes be enabled to acquirecertain
lands adjacent to the Hospital and forming part of the
lands of His Majesty'sPrison in the City and County
Borough of Belfast,and to use such landsforHospital
purposes .
And whereasthe landsof His Majesty'sPrisonin
the City and County Borough of Belfastare now vested
intheMinistryofHome AffairsforNorthernIreland(in
thisAct called" the Ministry" ).
And whereas it is expedientthat the Ministry
should be empowered to convey to the Hospital for
Hospitalpurposessuch part of the saidlandsforsuch
considerationand upon suchtermsand conditionsasmay
be prescribedby the Ministry.

CHAPTER ii.
An Act to empower the Lord Mayor ,Aldermen
and Citizens of the City of Belfast to provide
and work trolleyvehicles; to provide for the
disqualificationof members of the Council in
certainevents ;to make provisionforthe super-
annuation ofcertainofficersof the Corporation ;
to conferfurtherpowers upon the Corporation
with referenceto rating and publichealth ; and
to confervariousotherpowers upon the Corpora-
tion in relationto the good government of the
City ;and forotherpurposes. [17th June ,1930.]
WHEREAS the City of Belfast(in thisAct called
" the City" ) is a county borough subject to the
Acts relatingto MunicipalCorporationsin Northern
Irelandand the Lord Mayor ,Aldermen and Citizensof
the City (in thisAct called" the Corporation" ) acting
by the Council are the urban sanitaryauthorityfor the
district thereof :
And whereas the several local Acts and Orders
mentioned in the Schedule to this Act are in force within
the City,which Acts and Orders are in thisAct referred
to collectivelyas " the former Acts " and each of them
separatelyas an Act or Order of the year in which the
same was passed or made :
And whereas itisexpedient and willbe of public
and local advantage that the Corporation should be
empowered to provide and work trolleyvehicles:
And whereas itisexpedient that members of the
Councilshould be disqualifiedforholdingofficeincertain
events :
And whereas itisexpedient that provisionshould
be made in respect of the superannuation of certain
officersof the Corporation :
And whereas it isexpedient that there should be
conferred upon the Corporation further powers with
referenceto the ratingofcertaintenements and heredita-
ments in the City :

## Page 281

[20 & 21 GEO .5.] BelfastCorporationAct 275[Ch . ii.]
(NorthernIreland),1930.
And whereas itis expedient that there should be
conferredupon the Corporationfurtherpowers inrelation
to Public Health :
And whereas it is expedient that the present
limitationon the power ofthe Corporationto make a rate
for the purposes of The Public Parks (Ireland)Act ,1869
should be increasedto fourpencein the pound :
And whereas it is expedientthatfurtherpowers
should be conferredupon the Corporation with respect
to the good government and management of the City :
And whereas itisexpedient that the Corporation
should be empowered to raisemoney forthe purposes of
thisAct as in thisAct provided :
And whereas itisexpedientthattheotherprovisions
in this Act contained should be enacted :
And whereas the purposes of thisAct cannot be
effectedwithout the authorityof Parliament :
And whereas the consent of the Board of Trade to
this Act has been obtained in accordance with the
provisionsofsub-section(2)ofsectiontwo oftheNorthern
Ireland(MiscellaneousProvisions) Act,1928,passedby
the Parliament of the United Kingdom :
And whereas in relationto the promotion of the
BillforthisAct the requirementsof the Borough Funds
Acts (Northern Ireland) 1888 and 1928 have been
observed .
MAY IT THEREFORE PLEASE YOUR MAJESTY
That itmay be enacted and BE IT ENACTED by the

and by the authorityof the same as follows(that isto
say ) :-

CHAPTER iii.
An Act to extend the boundaries of the Larne
Urban District, to authorize the acquisitionof
markets , to make further provision as to col-
lectionof rates,to make furtherprovisionforthe
improvement and good government of the said
district,and for other purposes.
[25th November , 1930.]

Streets .

Council shallin any new streetcommence to erectany
